<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">2011 Korean FA Cup</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">

<p>The <b>2011 Korean FA Cup</b>, known as the <a href="/wiki/Hana_Financial_Group" title="Hana Financial Group">Hana Bank</a> <a href="/wiki/Korean_FA_Cup" title="Korean FA Cup">FA Cup</a> for sponsorship reasons, was the 16th edition of <a href="/wiki/Korean_FA_Cup" title="Korean FA Cup">Korean FA Cup</a>. 2011 KFA Cup began on 12 March 2011.</p>
<p>The cup winner were guaranteed a place in the <a href="/wiki/2012_AFC_Champions_League" title="2012 AFC Champions League">2012 AFC Champions League</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Participants">Participants</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_Korean_FA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Participants">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="K-League">K-League</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_Korean_FA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: K-League">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>All of K-League teams are entered in round of 32. Total 16 teams took part in 2011 KFA Cup.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Korea_National_League">Korea National League</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_Korean_FA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Korea National League">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Challengers_League">Challengers League</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_Korean_FA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Challengers League">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Only <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gyeongju_Citizen" title="Gyeongju Citizen">Gyeongju Citizen</a>, the winner of <a href="/wiki/2010_K3_League" title="2010 K3 League">2010 season</a>, was entered in second round and top nine team of <a href="/wiki/2010_K3_League" title="2010 K3 League">2010 season</a> are entered in first round. Other Challengers League teams don't take part in 2011 KFA Cup. Total nine teams of Challengers League took part in 2011 KFA Cup.</p>
<div>
<table class="multicol" role="presentation" style="border-collapse: collapse; padding: 0; border: 0; background:transparent; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td style="width:50%; text-align:left; vertical-align:top;">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bucheon_FC_1995" title="Bucheon FC 1995">Bucheon FC 1995</a> (First Round)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cheongju_Jikji_FC" title="Cheongju Jikji FC">Cheongju Jikji FC</a> (First Round)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gyeongju_Citizen_FC" title="Gyeongju Citizen FC">Gyeongju Citizen FC</a> (Second Round)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Icheon_Citizen_FC" title="Icheon Citizen FC">Icheon Citizen FC</a> (First Round)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jeonju_EM_FC" title="Jeonju EM FC">Jeonju EM FC</a> (First Round)</li>
</ul>
</td>
<td style="width:50%; text-align:left; vertical-align:top;">
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Namyangju_United" title="Namyangju United">Namyangju United</a> (First Round)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/FC_Pocheon" title="FC Pocheon">FC Pocheon</a> (First Round)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Seoul_United" title="Seoul United">Seoul United</a> (First Round)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yangju_Citizen_FC" title="Yangju Citizen FC">Yangju Citizen FC</a> (First Round)</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="University">University</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_Korean_FA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: University">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>All of university teams are entered in first round. Semifinalists of <a href="/wiki/2010_U-League" title="2010 U-League">2010 U-League</a> and several university football tournament winners took part in 2011 KFA Cup.</p>
<div>
<table class="multicol" role="presentation" style="border-collapse: collapse; padding: 0; border: 0; background:transparent; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td style="width:50%; text-align:left; vertical-align:top;">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yonsei_University" title="Yonsei University">Yonsei University</a> (<a href="/wiki/2010_U-League" title="2010 U-League">2010 U-League</a> champion)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kyunghee_University" title="Kyunghee University">Kyunghee University</a> (2010 U-League runner-up)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Honam_University" title="Honam University">Honam University</a> (2010 U-League semifinalist)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kwangwoon_University" title="Kwangwoon University">Kwangwoon University</a> (2010 U-League semifinalist)</li>
</ul>
</td>
<td style="width:50%; text-align:left; vertical-align:top;">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Korea_University" title="Korea University">Korea University</a> (2010 National University Football Championship 1st)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dongguk_University" title="Dongguk University">Dongguk University</a> (2010 Autumn College League Tournament 1st)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yeungnam_University" title="Yeungnam University">Yeungnam University</a> (2010 Spring College League Tournament 1st)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Konkuk_University" title="Konkuk University">Konkuk University</a> (2010 <a href="/wiki/Korean_National_Sports_Festival" title="Korean National Sports Festival">Korean National Sports Festival</a> University level winner)</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Results">Results</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_Korean_FA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Results">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preliminary_Round">Preliminary Round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_Korean_FA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Preliminary Round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Preliminary round is consist of two round. First round was held on 12 March 2011 and second round was held on 10 April 2011.</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="First_round">First round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_Korean_FA_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: First round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The draw for the first round was held on 10 February 2011.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></p>

</li>
<li>Top goalscorer : <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea"><img alt="South Korea" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/23px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/35px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/45px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Go_Seul-Ki" title="Go Seul-Ki">Go Seul-Ki</a> (<a href="/wiki/Ulsan_Hyundai_FC" title="Ulsan Hyundai FC">Ulsan Hyundai</a>, 4 goals)</li>
<li>Most Valuable Player : <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea"><img alt="South Korea" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/23px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/35px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/45px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cho_Dong-Geon" title="Cho Dong-Geon">Cho Dong-Geon</a> (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Seongnam_Ilhwa_Chunma" title="Seongnam Ilhwa Chunma">Seongnam Ilhwa Chunma</a>)</li>
</ul>
